224      "    match = re.search(\"(Dr|Mrs?|Ms|Miss|Master|Rev|Capt|Mlle|Col|Major|Sir|Jonkheer|Lady|the Countess|Mme|Don)\\\\.\",name)\n", 
225      "    if match:\n", 
226      "        title = match.group(0)\n", 
227      "        if (title == 'Don.' or title == 'Major.' or title == 'Capt.'):\n", 
228      "            title = 'Sir.'\n", 
229      "        if (title == 'Mlle.' or title == 'Mme.'):\n", 
230      "            title = 'Miss.'\n", 
231      "        return title\n", 
232      "    else:\n", 
233      "        return \"Other\"\n", 
234      "passengers[\"Title\"] = passengers[\"Name\"].apply(findTitle)\n", 
235      "passengers[\"Title\"].show()"
